{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Qis7R7tgD3p8DQYhKPbtoM","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"No results for IWL_DEV_INFO 0x3165 0x4010. So it seems that 0x3165 device 0x4010 entries are only in the PCI table, not in the dev_info table. This makes sense because the dev_info table is only for CONFIG_IWLMVM devices, and might not include all devices.\n\nLet me now check what is the correct approach. Since the bug report mentions \"missing PCI subdevice entries\", I should focus on the PCI table. Let me also check if there's a pattern with what configuration should be used for the missing entries.\n\nLooking at the pattern:- 0x2526, 0x0210 -> iwl9260_2ac_cfg (in PCI table)\n- 0x2526, 0x0214 -> iwl9260_2ac_cfg (in PCI table)- 0x2526, 0x1010 -> iwl9260_2ac_cfg (in PCI table)- 0x2526, 0x1210 -> iwl9260_2ac_cfg (in PCI table)- 0x2526, 0x0010, 0x0014, 0x0018, 0x001C -> iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg (in DEV_INFO table, not in PCI table)\n\nAnd:- 0x2526, 0x6010, 0x6014 -> iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg (in DEV_INFO table)- 0x2526, 0x8010, 0x8014 -> iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg (in DEV_INFO table)- 0x2526, 0xA014 -> iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg (in DEV_INFO table)- 0x2526, 0xE010, 0xE014 -> iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg (in DEV_INFO table)\n\n\nThe DEV_INFO table contains entries with subdevice IDs 0x0010, 0x0014, 0x0018, 0x001C, 0x6010, 0x6014, 0x8010, 0x8014, 0xA014, 0xE010, and 0xE014. The missing 0x4010, 0x4018, and 0x401C follow the same pattern and should map to iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg.\n\nNow I need to determine if these should also appear in the PCI table. Looking at what's actually there: 0x0210 and 0x0214 are in the PCI table but absent from DEV_INFO, while 0x1010 and 0x1210 follow the same pattern. This suggests a split where entries in the 0x00xx, 0x60xx, 0x80xx, 0xAx xx, and 0xExxx ranges belong in DEV_INFO, while those in other ranges like 0x02xx and 0x10xx go in the PCI table. The 0x4010, 0x4018, and 0x401C entries should probably follow the DEV_INFO pattern since they're in the 0x4xxx range.\n\nLooking at the PCI table structure, there's a catch-all entry using PCI_ANY_ID that acts as a fallback when specific subdevice IDs don't match. This means the DEV_INFO table provides device-specific configurations while the PCI table handles initial device matching. The missing entries likely need both: an entry in the PCI table for device recognition and corresponding entries in DEV_INFO with their specific configurations.\n\nThe firmware loading failure suggests the driver isn't recognizing the device at all, which points to a missing PCI table entry. Since there's already a generic 0x2526 entry with PCI_ANY_ID, devices like 0x4010 should theoretically be matched, but they're apparently not being loaded correctly, indicating the specific subdevice IDs need explicit entries in the DEV_INFO table to function properly.\n\nThe fix requires adding specific PCI table entries for 0x4010, 0x4018, and 0x401C mapped to iwl9260_2ac_cfg, with optional DEV_INFO entries using iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg for more granular configuration.
